If the source side matches, too, we\n\t\t// need to exclude inhibiting alerts for which the same is true.\n\t\tif inhibitedByFP, eq := r.hasEqual(lset, r.SourceMatchers.Matches(lset), now); eq {\n\t\t\tih.marker.SetInhibited(fp, inhibitedByFP.String())\n\t\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"alert inhibited\",\n\t\t\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n\t\t\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.inhibit_rule.source.fingerprint\", inhibitedByFP.String()),\n\t\t\t\t),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tih.marker.SetInhibited(fp)\n\tspan.AddEvent(\"alert not inhibited\")\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// An InhibitRule specifies that a class of (source) alerts should inhibit\n// notifications for another class of (target) alerts if all specified matching\n// labels are equal between the two alerts. This may be used to inhibit alerts\n// from sending notifications if their meaning is logically a subset of a\n// higher-level alert.\ntype InhibitRule struct {\n\t// Name is an optional name for the inhibition rule.\n\tName string\n\t// The set of Filters which define the group of source alerts (which inhibit\n\t// the target alerts).\n\tSourceMatchers labels.Matchers\n\t// The set of Filters which define the group of target alerts (which are\n\t// inhibited by the source alerts).\n\tTargetMatchers labels.Matchers\n\t// A set of label names whose label values need to be identical in source and\n\t// target alerts in order for the inhibition to take effect.\n\tEqual map[model.LabelName]struct{}\n\n\t// Cache of alerts matching source labels.\n\tscache *store.Alerts\n\n\t// Index of fingerprints of source alert equal labels to fingerprint of source alert.\n\t// The index helps speed up source alert lookups from scache significantely in scenarios with 100s of source alerts cached.\n\t// The index items might overwrite eachother if multiple source alerts have exact equal labels.\n\t// Overwrites only happen if the new source alert has bigger EndsAt value.\n\tsindex *index\n}\n\n// NewInhibitRule returns a new InhibitRule based on a configuration definition.","numLines":150,"startLine":100,"totalLines":402}}}

Prometheus Alertmanager notification pipeline flows through these key stages:\\n\\n**1. Alert Ingestion (api/v2/api.go)**\\nAlerts arrive via HTTP POST to the `postAlertsHandler` function which parses OpenAPI alert models, validates them, and calls `api.alerts.Put()` to store them in the alert provider.\\n\\n**2. Alert Provider Storage (provider/mem/mem.go)**\\nThe `Put` method stores alerts in an in-memory provider and broadcasts them through a subscription mechanism, allowing the dispatcher to receive alert updates.\\n\\n**3. Routing Tree Traversal (dispatch/dispatch.go and dispatch/route.go)**\\nWhen alerts are received, `Dispatcher.routeAlert()` matches the alert against the routing tree using `Route.Match()`. The `Match` method performs a depth-first left-to-right search through the routing tree hierarchy, returning all matching routes. Each alert can match multiple routes based on matchers defined in the configuration.\\n\\n**4. Aggregation and Grouping (dispatch/dispatch.go)**\\nFor each matching route, `groupAlert()` creates or updates an aggregation group (stored in `aggrGroup` struct). Alerts are grouped by labels specified in the route's GroupBy configuration. The grouping happens before the notification pipeline.\\n\\n**5. Inhibition Check (inhibit/inhibit.go)**\\nInhibition rules are checked in the notification pipeline through the `Inhibitor.Mutes()` method. The Inhibitor maintains a cache of source alerts matching inhibition rule criteria. When checking if an alert should be muted, it verifies if any inhibition rule's source alerts match and if the target labels equal the specified label set.\\n\\n**6. Silence Check (silence/silence.go)**\\nSilences are checked through the `Silencer.Mutes()` method. The Silencer queries active/pending silences using `Silences.Query()` and checks if the alert labels match the silence matchers. It maintains a cache to avoid redundant queries.\\n\\n**7. Notification Pipeline Construction (notify/notify.go)**\\nThe `PipelineBuilder.New()` method constructs a multi-stage pipeline for each receiver:\\n- `GossipSettleStage`: Waits for cluster state synchronization\\n- `MuteStage` (inhibition): Applies inhibition check using the Inhibitor\\n- `TimeActiveStage`/`TimeMuteStage`: Checks time intervals\\n- `MuteStage` (silence): Applies silence check using the Silencer  \\n- Receiver stage with:\\n  - `WaitStage`: Waits for group interval\\n  - `DedupStage`: Filters duplicate notifications\\n  - `RetryStage`: Handles retries with backoff\\n  - `SetNotifiesStage`: Records sent notifications\\n  - `Integration.Notify`: Sends to actual receiver (Slack, PagerDuty, etc.)\\n\\n**8. Final Dispatch (dispatch/dispatch.go and notify/notify.go)**\\nThe `aggrGroup.run()` method manages the aggregation group lifecycle, periodically flushing alerts through the notification pipeline. Alerts flow through all pipeline stages sequentially, with each stage potentially filtering alerts before passing them to the next stage. Finally, `Integration.Notify()` sends the alerts to the configured notification receivers.\\n\\nThe entire pipeline is tracing-enabled with OpenTelemetry spans at each critical stage for observability.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1669,"cache_read_input_tokens":65859,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1669},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3d1eea5f-8601-4e92-a8fc-1b481bacc02b","uuid":"23934b6a-bbef-41dd-9845-aabd9138b786"}

Prometheus Alertmanager notification pipeline flows through these key stages:\\n\\n**1. Alert Ingestion (api/v2/api.go)**\\nAlerts arrive via HTTP POST to the `postAlertsHandler` function which parses OpenAPI alert models, validates them, and calls `api.alerts.Put()` to store them in the alert provider.\\n\\n**2. Alert Provider Storage (provider/mem/mem.go)**\\nThe `Put` method stores alerts in an in-memory provider and broadcasts them through a subscription mechanism, allowing the dispatcher to receive alert updates.\\n\\n**3. Routing Tree Traversal (dispatch/dispatch.go and dispatch/route.go)**\\nWhen alerts are received, `Dispatcher.routeAlert()` matches the alert against the routing tree using `Route.Match()`. The `Match` method performs a depth-first left-to-right search through the routing tree hierarchy, returning all matching routes. Each alert can match multiple routes based on matchers defined in the configuration.\\n\\n**4. Aggregation and Grouping (dispatch/dispatch.go)**\\nFor each matching route, `groupAlert()` creates or updates an aggregation group (stored in `aggrGroup` struct). Alerts are grouped by labels specified in the route's GroupBy configuration. The grouping happens before the notification pipeline.\\n\\n**5. Inhibition Check (inhibit/inhibit.go)**\\nInhibition rules are checked in the notification pipeline through the `Inhibitor.Mutes()` method. The Inhibitor maintains a cache of source alerts matching inhibition rule criteria. When checking if an alert should be muted, it verifies if any inhibition rule's source alerts match and if the target labels equal the specified label set.\\n\\n**6. Silence Check (silence/silence.go)**\\nSilences are checked through the `Silencer.Mutes()` method. The Silencer queries active/pending silences using `Silences.Query()` and checks if the alert labels match the silence matchers. It maintains a cache to avoid redundant queries.\\n\\n**7. Notification Pipeline Construction (notify/notify.go)**\\nThe `PipelineBuilder.New()` method constructs a multi-stage pipeline for each receiver:\\n- `GossipSettleStage`: Waits for cluster state synchronization\\n- `MuteStage` (inhibition): Applies inhibition check using the Inhibitor\\n- `TimeActiveStage`/`TimeMuteStage`: Checks time intervals\\n- `MuteStage` (silence): Applies silence check using the Silencer  \\n- Receiver stage with:\\n  - `WaitStage`: Waits for group interval\\n  - `DedupStage`: Filters duplicate notifications\\n  - `RetryStage`: Handles retries with backoff\\n  - `SetNotifiesStage`: Records sent notifications\\n  - `Integration.Notify`: Sends to actual receiver (Slack, PagerDuty, etc.)\\n\\n**8. Final Dispatch (dispatch/dispatch.go and notify/notify.go)**\\nThe `aggrGroup.run()` method manages the aggregation group lifecycle, periodically flushing alerts through the notification pipeline. Alerts flow through all pipeline stages sequentially, with each stage potentially filtering alerts before passing them to the next stage. Finally, `Integration.Notify()` sends the alerts to the configured notification receivers.\\n\\nThe entire pipeline is tracing-enabled with OpenTelemetry spans at each critical stage for observability.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
